It's pretty obvious that the stretching out and insertion of irrelevant plotlines is because Favreau stole the first two episodes of Season 3 and inserted them in Book of Boba Fett.   They wanted a full 8-episode season, but the overall plot was already set, with pre-production done and episodes being filmed, so the filler material couldn't tie-in with the existing plotlines -- hence the clone doctor story that went-nowhere-did-nothing and the absurdly stupid malfunctioning droid story.   But since those two episodes also needed to steal some scenes from existing episodes to blend in, that meant they had to shoot additional filler scenes to take their place in the other episodes, so you got scenes with pointless time-wasting conversations inserted.   In short: blame Kathleen Kennedy for screwing up Book of Boba Fett for how Mando season 3 turned out.

This show is about a super cool bounty hunter, who wears shiny armor like a boss, and goes on all sorts of crazy missions across the galaxy.  But the real star of the show is the cutest little green alien you've ever seen, Baby Yoda! He's so adorable, with those big eyes and pointy ears, and he's always getting into trouble. I mean, who wouldn't want to protect this little guy with their life?  And let's not forget about all the epic action scenes, like when the Mandalorian fights those giant monsters, or when he takes on a whole gang of bad guys single-handedly. It's like watching a video game come to life!  So, if you're a true Star Wars fan, you need to watch The Mandalorian ASAP. And if you're not already a fan, well, you will be after watching this show.
